#######################################################################################
VERSION 1.6
#######################################################################################

CHANGES -------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* Replaced STEREO versions of 3D positional sounds with MONO versions This makes it
  better for use in games where 3D positional audio is better as mono files instead of
  stereo and it also saves space. The sounds were originally intended to be released as
  MONO samples but were incorrectly saved as stereo.
  UI sounds, ambiences, and music effects remain as stereo audio.
  
* Some minor changes to category folder names and a few sounds have moved

ADDED 3087 SOUNDS ---------------------------------------------------------------------

CHANGES -------------------------------------------------------------------------------
* For UE4 compatibility (and other engines/environments):
  - Removed & from folder names (replaced with _)
  - Removed space from folder names (replaced with _)
  - Removed brackets "()" from file names.
* Added MetaData (Broadcast Wave) including keywords to all sound effects
* Converted some files that were in the wrong bit-rate & frequency
* Removed spelling errors in some files
